function AD takes nothing returns nothing
local trigger UD
local playerunitevent ID
local integer PD
set Gi=CreateTrigger()
set UD=Gi
set ID=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_RESEARCH_FINISH
set PD=0
loop
call TriggerRegisterPlayerUnitEvent(UD,Player(PD),ID,null)
set PD=PD+1
exitwhen PD==bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS
endloop
call TriggerAddCondition(Gi,Condition(Fa))
call TriggerAddAction(Gi,ka)
set UD=null
set ID=null
endfunction

endfunction

set Xt=CreateTrigger()
set XU=Xt
set CU=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_RESEARCH_FINISH
set VU=0
loop
call TriggerRegisterPlayerUnitEvent(XU,Player(VU),CU,null)
set VU=VU+1
exitwhen VU==bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS
endloop
call TriggerAddCondition(Xt,Condition(fq))
call TriggerAddAction(Xt,Rq)
set XU=null
set CU=null
endfunction

function PL takes nothing returns boolean
if GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit())!=1747988809 then
return false
endif
return true
endfunction
function AL takes nothing returns boolean
if not PL() then
return false
endif
return true
endfunction
function h0w takes integer g0w returns string
if g0w==0 then
return "|cffADADADtrace|r"
elseif g0w==1 then
return "|cff2685DCdebug|r"
elseif g0w==2 then
return "|cffFFCC00info|r"
elseif g0w==3 then
return "|cffF47E3Ewarning|r"
elseif g0w==4 then
return "|cffFB2700error|r"
endif
return "?"
endfunction
function c4 takes string B1,string N1 returns nothing
local integer M1
local integer w4
local integer u4
local string r4
local integer s4
local integer t4
local string i4
local string S4
set Lb[Kb]=N1
set Kb=Kb+1
set M1=StringHash(B1)
if HaveSavedInteger(cc,-1,M1) then
if LoadInteger(cc,-1,M1)+60<nc then
set i4=B1
set N1=""
set w4=Kb
set u4=0
loop
set w4=w4-1
set u4=u4+1
exitwhen u4>20 or w4<0
set N1=N1+"\n   "+Lb[w4]
endloop

call SaveBoolean(cc,-1,M1,true)
endif
else
call SaveInteger(cc,-1,M1,R2I(nc))
set S4="Message: "+B1

set s4=Kb
set t4=0
loop

set t4=t4+1

endfunction

function Yqw takes string Rqw returns integer
local integer Tqw
set Lb[Kb]=Rqw
set Kb=Kb+1
set Lb[Kb]="when calling alloc_Table in Table, line 5"
set Kb=Kb+1
if AO==0 then
if DO<32768 then
set DO=DO+1
set Tqw=DO
set HO[Tqw]=728
else
call c4("Out of memory: Could not create Table.","when calling error in Table, line 6")
set Tqw=0
endif
else
set AO=AO-1
set Tqw=PO[AO]
set HO[Tqw]=728
endif
set Kb=Kb-1-1
return Tqw
endfunction
function initializeTable takes string stackPos returns nothing

endif
endif

set i_2=i_2+1
endloop
set Kb=Kb-1
endfunction

function AN takes playercolor kN returns integer

set xN=0
set vN=0
endif
set Xb=jN

set Vb=vN
set mN=null
set ZN=null
return Xb
endfunction

function Im takes nothing returns nothing
local player Fm=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
local playerstate km=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER
local playerstate jm
local playerstate xm
local player vm
local force mm
local location Qm
local real Wm
local real Em
local player Zm
local force Um
if km==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set jm=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Fm,jm,GetPlayerState(Fm,jm)+500)
elseif km==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set xm=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Fm,xm,GetPlayerState(Fm,xm)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(Fm,km,GetPlayerState(Fm,km)+500)
set vm=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
set mm=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(mm,vm)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),mm) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_084")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
set Zm=GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())
set Um=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Um,Zm)
set Qm=y
set Wm=GetLocationX(Qm)
set Em=GetLocationY(Qm)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Um) then
call PingMinimap(Wm,Em,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Fm=null
set km=null
set jm=null
set xm=null
set vm=null
set mm=null
set Qm=null
set Zm=null
set Um=null
endfunction

function f5 takes real e5,real q5,real a5,real n5,real d5 returns real

endfunction

function gsw takes integer osw,string Osw returns nothing

local boolean fsw

local real Ysw
local real Gsw
set Lb[Kb]=Osw

endif

endif
call SetUnitState(lsw,UNIT_STATE_LIFE,GetUnitState(lsw,UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE)*RMaxBJ(0.,60.0)*0.01)
call SetUnitState(lsw,UNIT_STATE_MANA,GetUnitState(lsw,UNIT_STATE_MAX_MANA)*RMaxBJ(0.,0.0)*0.01)

endfunction

return D0w
endfunction

function fuw takes unit puw,unit euw returns real
local real quw=GetUnitX(puw)
local real auw=GetUnitY(puw)
local real nuw=quw-GetUnitX(euw)
local real duw=auw-GetUnitY(euw)
return SquareRoot(nuw*nuw+duw*duw)
endfunction

function Kk takes nothing returns nothing
local player Qk=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())

elseif Wk==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set Zk=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Qk,Zk,GetPlayerState(Qk,Zk)+250)
endif

call ForceAddPlayer(Ik,Uk)

call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1229")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())

set Jk=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Jk,Hk)
set Pk=y
set Ak=GetLocationX(Pk)
set Dk=GetLocationY(Pk)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Jk) then
call PingMinimap(Ak,Dk,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Qk=null
set Wk=null
set Ek=null
set Zk=null
set Uk=null
set Ik=null
set Pk=null
set Hk=null
set Jk=null
endfunction

function Nj takes nothing returns nothing
local player Pj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())

local playerstate Hj

local real Cj

set Dj=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Pj,Dj,GetPlayerState(Pj,Dj)+500)
elseif Aj==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set Hj=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Pj,Hj,GetPlayerState(Pj,Hj)+500)
endif

call ForceAddPlayer(Kj,Jj)

call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1231")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())

call ForceAddPlayer(Bj,Vj)
set Lj=y

set Cj=GetLocationY(Lj)

call PingMinimap(Xj,Cj,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Pj=null
set Aj=null
set Dj=null
set Hj=null
set Jj=null
set Kj=null
set Lj=null
set Vj=null
set Bj=null
endfunction

function Rm takes nothing returns nothing
local player Om=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
local playerstate lm=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD
local playerstate bm
local playerstate ym
local player pm
local force em
local location qm
local real am
local real nm
local player dm
local force fm
if lm==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set bm=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Om,bm,GetPlayerState(Om,bm)+500)
elseif lm==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set ym=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Om,ym,GetPlayerState(Om,ym)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(Om,lm,GetPlayerState(Om,lm)+500)
set pm=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
set em=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(em,pm)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),em) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_083")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
set dm=GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())
set fm=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(fm,dm)
set qm=y
set am=GetLocationX(qm)
set nm=GetLocationY(qm)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),fm) then
call PingMinimap(am,nm,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Om=null
set lm=null
set bm=null
set ym=null
set pm=null
set em=null
set qm=null
set dm=null
set fm=null
endfunction

endfunction

function bG takes nothing returns nothing
local player SG=GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker())
local player cG=GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker())
local player oG
local player OG
local unit lG
set r[GetPlayerId(SG)+1]=r[GetPlayerId(cG)+1]+1

set OG=GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())
set r[GetPlayerId(oG)+1]=r[GetPlayerId(OG)+1]-1
call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(),GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()),bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_DEFAULTS)
call SetUnitOwner(bj_lastReplacedUnit,GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()),true)
set lG=GetTriggerUnit()
call SetUnitState(lG,UNIT_STATE_LIFE,GetUnitState(lG,UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE)*RMaxBJ(0.,100.)*0.01)
set SG=null
set cG=null
set oG=null
set OG=null
set lG=null
endfunction

function bj takes nothing returns nothing
local player wj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate uj=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER
local playerstate rj
local playerstate sj
local player tj
local force ij
local location Sj
local real cj
local real oj
local player Oj
local force lj
if uj==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set rj=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(wj,rj,GetPlayerState(wj,rj)+500)
elseif uj==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set sj=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(wj,sj,GetPlayerState(wj,sj)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(wj,uj,GetPlayerState(wj,uj)+500)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set tj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set ij=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(ij,tj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),ij) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1228")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set Oj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set lj=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(lj,Oj)
set Sj=y
set cj=GetLocationX(Sj)
set oj=GetLocationY(Sj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),lj) then
call PingMinimap(cj,oj,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set wj=null
set uj=null
set rj=null
set sj=null
set tj=null
set ij=null
set Sj=null
set Oj=null
set lj=null
endfunction

function cK takes nothing returns nothing
local integer wK=1
local integer uK=1751343475
local player rK=GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())
local rect SK=bj_mapInitialPlayableArea
local location iK=Location(GetRectCenterX(SK),GetRectCenterY(SK))
local location sK=Location(GetLocationX(iK)+100000000.00,GetLocationY(iK)+100000000.00)
local real tK=bj_UNIT_FACING
call GroupClear(bj_lastCreatedGroup)
loop
set wK=wK-1
exitwhen wK<0
call CreateUnitAtLocSaveLast(rK,uK,sK,tK)
call GroupAddUnit(bj_lastCreatedGroup,bj_lastCreatedUnit)
endloop
call ShowUnit(bj_lastCreatedUnit,false)
set rK=null
set sK=null
set iK=null
set SK=null
endfunction

set wh=null
set sh=null
set th=null
set ih=null
endfunction

function vj takes nothing returns nothing
local player fj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate Rj=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD
local playerstate Tj
local playerstate Yj
local player Gj
local force gj
local location hj
local real Fj
local real kj
local player jj
local force xj
if Rj==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set Tj=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(fj,Tj,GetPlayerState(fj,Tj)+250)
elseif Rj==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set Yj=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(fj,Yj,GetPlayerState(fj,Yj)+250)
endif
call SetPlayerState(fj,Rj,GetPlayerState(fj,Rj)+250)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set Gj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set gj=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(gj,Gj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),gj) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1230")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set jj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set xj=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(xj,jj)
set hj=y
set Fj=GetLocationX(hj)
set kj=GetLocationY(hj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),xj) then
call PingMinimap(Fj,kj,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set fj=null
set Rj=null
set Tj=null
set Yj=null
set Gj=null
set gj=null
set hj=null
set jj=null
set xj=null
endfunction

function Orw takes string Muw returns boolean

endif

set ub[PS[Ml[srw]]]=srw
set wb[srw]=PS[Ml[srw]]
endif
set PS[Ml[srw]]=srw
set Kb=Kb-1
set wrw=CreateTrigger()
set irw=GetWorldBounds()
set Srw=CreateRegion()
call RegionAddRect(Srw,irw)
call TriggerRegisterEnterRegion(wrw,Srw,null)
call TriggerAddAction(wrw,Mf)
set rrw=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH
set Lb[Kb]="when calling alloc_Upkeep_EventListener_line28 in Upkeep, line 28"
set Kb=Kb+1
if SO==0 then

function VC takes string mC returns boolean
local trigger QC
local playerunitevent WC
local playerunitevent EC
local integer ZC
local integer UC
local player IC
local location PC
local real AC
local integer DC
local integer HC
local trigger JC
local playerunitevent KC
local integer LC
local integer XC
local integer CC
set Lb[Kb]=mC
set Kb=Kb+1
if kc then
set ZC=5
set UC=1747988553
set IC=ro[0]
set PC=Location(-3000.0,1700.0)
set AC=0.
call GroupClear(bj_lastCreatedGroup)
loop
set ZC=ZC-1
exitwhen ZC<0
call CreateUnitAtLocSaveLast(IC,UC,PC,AC)
call GroupAddUnit(bj_lastCreatedGroup,bj_lastCreatedUnit)
endloop
endif
set WC=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SELECTED
set Lb[Kb]="when calling alloc_CityManage_EventListener_line9 in CityManage, line 9"
set Kb=Kb+1
if SO==0 then
if cO<32768 then
set cO=cO+1
set DC=cO
set oO[DC]=665
else
call c4("Out of memory: Could not create CityManage_EventListener_line9.","when calling error in CityManage, line 9")
set DC=0
endif
else
set SO=SO-1
set DC=iO[SO]
set oO[DC]=665
endif
set Kb=Kb-1
set Ml[DC]=0
set wb[DC]=0
set ub[DC]=0
set Lb[Kb]="when calling add in CityManage, line 9"
set Kb=Kb+1
set Lb[Kb]="when calling toIntId in ClosureEvents, line 112"
set Kb=Kb+1
set HC=ES[GetHandleId(WC)]
if HC==0 then
set HC=yB(WC,"when calling registerEventId in ClosureEvents, line 229")
endif
set Kb=Kb-1
set Ml[DC]=HC
if PS[Ml[DC]]!=0 then
set ub[PS[Ml[DC]]]=DC
set wb[DC]=PS[Ml[DC]]
endif
set PS[Ml[DC]]=DC
set Kb=Kb-1
set QC=CreateTrigger()
call TriggerAddCondition(QC,Condition(Ef))
call TriggerAddAction(QC,Zf)
set JC=QC
set KC=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST
set LC=0
loop
call TriggerRegisterPlayerUnitEvent(JC,Player(LC),KC,null)
set LC=LC+1
exitwhen LC==bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS
endloop
set EC=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED
set Lb[Kb]="when calling alloc_CityManage_EventListener_line33 in CityManage, line 33"
set Kb=Kb+1
if SO==0 then
if cO<32768 then
set cO=cO+1
set XC=cO
set oO[XC]=664
else
call c4("Out of memory: Could not create CityManage_EventListener_line33.","when calling error in CityManage, line 33")
set XC=0
endif
else
set SO=SO-1
set XC=iO[SO]
set oO[XC]=664
endif
set Kb=Kb-1
set Ml[XC]=0
set wb[XC]=0
set ub[XC]=0
set Lb[Kb]="when calling add in CityManage, line 33"
set Kb=Kb+1
set Lb[Kb]="when calling toIntId in ClosureEvents, line 112"
set Kb=Kb+1
set CC=ES[GetHandleId(EC)]
if CC==0 then
set CC=yB(EC,"when calling registerEventId in ClosureEvents, line 229")
endif
set Kb=Kb-1
set Ml[XC]=CC
if PS[Ml[XC]]!=0 then
set ub[PS[Ml[XC]]]=XC
set wb[XC]=PS[Ml[XC]]
endif
set PS[Ml[XC]]=XC
set Kb=Kb-1-1
set QC=null
set WC=null
set EC=null
set IC=null
set PC=null
set JC=null
set KC=null
return true
endfunction
